INNER JOIN [Projects] AS [p] ON [t].[ProjectId] = [p].[Id]
INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a] ON [t].[AssignedUserId] = [a].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t2].[Name], [t0].[TagId], [t0].[TaskId], [t2].[Id]
    FROM [TaskTags] AS [t0]
    INNER JOIN [Tags] AS [t2] ON [t0].[TagId] = [t2].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[TaskId]
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM [ProjectUsers] AS [p0]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = [p0].[ProjectId] AND [p0].[UserId] = @__currentUserId_0)
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [p].[Id], [a].[Id], [t1].[TagId], [t1].[TaskId]
